			[data-astro-transition=back][data-astro-transition-fallback="new"][data-astro-transition-scope="astro-36ssibgs-5"] { 
	animation-duration: 180ms;
	animation-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.76, 0, 0.24, 1);
	animation-fill-mode: both;
	animation-name: astroFadeIn; }</style></head> <body class="astro-sckkx6r4"> <div class="conference-wrapper border-b border-skin-line bg-skin-fill px-4 py-3 text-center text-skin-base astro-z2v4rtzb"><div class="mx-auto flex max-w-3xl flex-col items-center justify-center gap-3 sm:flex-row sm:gap-4 astro-z2v4rtzb"><div class="text-center sm:text-left astro-z2v4rtzb"><p class="text-lg font-semibold astro-z2v4rtzb"><span class="pulse-dot astro-z2v4rtzb"></span>

</svg><span class="astro-vj4tpspi">Go back</span> </button> </div> <main data-pagefind-body id="main-content" class="relative astro-vj4tpspi"> <h1 class="post-title astro-vj4tpspi" data-astro-transition-scope="astro-plk3gbjq-1">Building a Real-Time Todo App with Jazz and Vue 3</h1> <div class="my-2 flex items-center justify-between astro-vj4tpspi"> <div class="flex items-center space-x-2 opacity-80"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="scale-100 inline-block h-6 w-6 min-w-[1.375rem] fill-skin-base" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M7 11h2v2H7zm0 4h2v2H7zm4-4h2v2h-2zm0 4h2v2h-2zm4-4h2v2h-2zm0 4h2v2h-2z"></path><path d="M5 22h14c1.103 0 2-.897 2-2V6c0-1.103-.897-2-2-2h-2V2h-2v2H9V2H7v2H5c-1.103 0-2 .897-2 2v14c0 1.103.897 2 2 2zM19 8l.001 12H5V8h14z"></path></svg><span class="sr-only">Published:</span><span class="italic text-base"><time dateTime="2026-03-07T00:00:00.000Z">Mar 7, 2026</time><span class="sr-only"> at </span></span></div> <script>(()=>{var e=async t=>{await(await t())()};(self.Astro||(self.Astro={})).load=e;window.dispatchEvent(new Event("astro:load"));})();</script><astro-island uid="y7qqa" prefix="r3" component-url="/_astro/PostCopyButton.-PGtk4At.js" component-export="default" renderer-url="/_astro/client.DGA1VMK9.js" props="{&quot;title&quot;:[0,&quot;Building a Real-Time Todo App with Jazz and Vue 3&quot;],&quot;content&quot;:[0,&quot;import Aside from \&quot;@features/mdx-components/components/Aside.astro\&quot;;\nimport InternalLink from \&quot;@features/mdx-components/components/InternalLink.astro\&quot;;\nimport FileTree from \&quot;@features/filetree/components/FileTree.astro\&quot;;\nimport JazzCounterDemo from \&quot;@features/jazz-demo/components/JazzCounterDemo.astro\&quot;;\nimport JazzTodoDemo from \&quot;@features/jazz-demo/components/JazzTodoDemo.astro\&quot;;\nimport FractionalIndexingVisualizer from \&quot;@features/jazz-demo/components/FractionalIndexingVisualizer\&quot;;\nimport CoMapVisualizer from \&quot;@features/jazz-demo/components/CoMapVisualizer\&quot;;\nimport ExcalidrawSVG from \&quot;@features/mdx-components/components/ExcalidrawSVG.astro\&quot;;\nimport covalueOverview from \&quot;@assets/excalidraw/building-real-time-todo-app-jazz-vue/covalue-overview.svg?raw\&quot;;\nimport roleHierarchy from \&quot;@assets/excalidraw/building-real-time-todo-app-jazz-vue/role-hierarchy.svg?raw\&quot;;\nimport rolePermissionCheck from \&quot;@assets/excalidraw/building-real-time-todo-app-jazz-vue/role-permission-check.svg?raw\&quot;;\nimport groupPermissions from \&quot;@assets/excalidraw/building-real-time-todo-app-jazz-vue/group-permissions.svg?raw\&quot;;\nimport YouTube from \&quot;@features/mdx-components/components/YouTube.astro\&quot;;\n\n## TLDR\n\nBuild a real-time, offline-capable todo app with Jazz and Vue 3. Jazz replaces your entire backend with collaborative data structures called CoValues. Combined with `community-jazz-vue`, you get composables like `useCoState` that plug into Vue&#39;s reactivity system. The app syncs across tabs and devices, supports drag-and-drop with fractional indexing, and generates shareable URLs.\n\n## Why Jazz Replaces Your Entire Backend\n\nYou want real-time collaboration, offline support, and shareable URLs. In a traditional stack, that means building a sync server, a conflict resolution strategy, a permissions layer, and an API. Jazz collapses all of that into collaborative data structures called CoValues.\n\nThink of Vue&#39;s `ref` — it keeps the virtual DOM in sync with the real DOM. CoValues take that further: they sync your data across devices, across users, and across network boundaries. You mutate data locally, Jazz handles the rest.\n\n&lt;ExcalidrawSVG src={covalueOverview} alt=\&quot;CoValue overview showing how you mutate locally and Jazz automatically handles sync via real-time CRDT merge, persistence via IndexedDB with offline-first support, and security via Groups, roles, and E2E encryption\&quot; maxWidth=\&quot;520px\&quot; /&gt;\n\nThis is the next post in my local-first series, and it covers how to build a complete Vue 3 app on top of Jazz. You can find the official Jazz documentation at [jazz.tools](https://jazz.tools/).\n\nCombined with `community-jazz-vue`, a community-maintained Vue binding, you get composables like `useCoState` and a provider component that plug directly into Vue&#39;s reactivity system.\n\nIf you&#39;re new to local-first, start with the first post in this series:\n\n&lt;InternalLink slug=\&quot;what-is-local-first-web-development\&quot; /&gt;\n\nFor comparison, here&#39;s the same app built with Dexie.js and IndexedDB:\n\n&lt;InternalLink slug=\&quot;building-local-first-apps-vue-dexie\&quot; /&gt;\n\nAlso worth watching: Anselm Eickhoff, the creator of Jazz, gave a great workshop on local-first at VueConf 2025 where he live-coded with Jazz:\n\n&lt;YouTube id=\&quot;tPzHi9QiPcw\&quot; title=\&quot;Local-First with Vue and Jazz — Anselm Eickhoff at VueConf 2025\&quot; caption=\&quot;Anselm Eickhoff live vibe-coding a local-first app with Jazz and Vue at VueConf 2025\&quot; /&gt;\n\n## Your First CoValue: A Synced Counter\n\nVue&#39;s `ref` keeps the virtual DOM in sync with the real DOM — you update a `ref`, Vue re-renders. That&#39;s reactive state within one browser tab. Jazz&#39;s `useCoState` takes that same idea a step further: it keeps your data in sync across devices, across users, and across network boundaries. You mutate locally, Jazz propagates the change to every connected peer.\n\nThe simplest CoValue is a single field:\n\n```ts\nimport { co, z } from \&quot;jazz-tools\&quot;;\n\nconst Counter = co.map({ count: z.number() });\n```\n\nThat&#39;s one line of schema. Now subscribe to it in a Vue component:\n\n```vue\n&lt;script setup lang=\&quot;ts\&quot;&gt;\nimport { ref } from \&quot;vue\&quot;;\nimport { useCoState } from \&quot;community-jazz-vue\&quot;;\nimport { Counter } from \&quot;./schema\&quot;;\n\n// Create a counter and grab its ID\nconst counterId = ref&lt;string | undefined&gt;();\nconst newCounter = Counter.create({ count: 0 });\ncounterId.value = newCounter.$jazz.id;\n\n// Subscribe — returns a reactive ref that updates on local and remote changes\nconst counter = useCoState(Counter, counterId);\n\nfunction increment() {\n  if (counter.value?.$isLoaded) {\n    counter.value.$jazz.set(\&quot;count\&quot;, (counter.value.count ?? 0) + 1);\n  }\n}\n\nfunction decrement() {\n  if (counter.value?.$isLoaded) {\n    counter.value.$jazz.set(\&quot;count\&quot;, Math.max(0, (counter.value.count ?? 0) - 1));\n  }\n}\n&lt;/script&gt;\n\n&lt;template&gt;\n  &lt;div v-if=\&quot;!counter?.$isLoaded\&quot;&gt;Loading...&lt;/div&gt;\n  &lt;div v-else&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;{{ counter.count }}&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;button @click=\&quot;decrement\&quot;&gt;−&lt;/button&gt;\n    &lt;button @click=\&quot;increment\&quot;&gt;+&lt;/button&gt;\n  &lt;/div&gt;\n&lt;/template&gt;\n```\n\nThree things are happening here:\n\n1. `Counter.create({ count: 0 })` creates a new CoValue instance and persists it locally.\n2. `useCoState(Counter, counterId)` subscribes to that CoValue. It returns a reactive `Ref` that starts unloaded, populates once available, and re-renders on every change — just like Vue&#39;s `ref`, but across the network.\n3. `$jazz.set(\&quot;count\&quot;, ...)` mutates the CoValue directly. No API call, no action dispatch — Jazz syncs the change to all connected peers.\n\nThis already works for a single user. But there&#39;s a problem: **by default, CoValues are private**. Only the creator can read or write them. If you shared this counter&#39;s ID with another user, they&#39;d get nothing — the CoValue is invisible to them.\n\n### Making It Shareable with Groups\n\nTo let others access the counter, you need a **Group**. Groups are how Jazz controls who gets access and what they can do. Every CoValue has an owner — either an Account (private) or a Group (shared).\n\n```ts\nimport { Group } from \&quot;jazz-tools\&quot;;\n\nconst group = Group.create();\ngroup.addMember(\&quot;everyone\&quot;, \&quot;writer\&quot;);\nconst newCounter = Counter.create({ count: 0 }, { owner: group });\n```\n\nThat&#39;s three lines. `Group.create()` makes a new permission group. `addMember(\&quot;everyone\&quot;, \&quot;writer\&quot;)` grants public write access — the `\&quot;everyone\&quot;` keyword is a special shorthand that includes all users, even anonymous guests. Passing `{ owner: group }` to `Counter.create` assigns the counter to that group instead of the default private account.\n\nNow anyone who knows the CoValue ID can read and write the same counter. No API keys, no auth server — sharing the ID is all it takes.\n\nTry it — click the + button in one panel and watch the count update in the other. Both panels are independent Jazz clients syncing via Jazz Cloud:\n\n&lt;JazzCounterDemo /&gt;\n\n&lt;Aside type=\&quot;info\&quot;&gt;\nThe `\&quot;everyone\&quot;` + `\&quot;writer\&quot;` combination is intentionally permissive — great for demos and public collaboration. For real apps, Jazz supports granular roles (`reader`, `writer`, `admin`) and per-user membership. We&#39;ll use the same pattern for the todo app below.\n&lt;/Aside&gt;\n\nThat&#39;s the entire model: define your data with `co.map`, subscribe with `useCoState`, mutate directly. But we glossed over something important — how does Jazz decide who can access a CoValue, and what stops someone from escalating their own permissions?\n\n## How Jazz Permissions Work\n\nThe counter example used `addMember(\&quot;everyone\&quot;, \&quot;writer\&quot;)` to make data publicly accessible. Let&#39;s look at what&#39;s happening under the hood.\n\nJazz defines a role hierarchy where each role includes the permissions of the roles below it:\n\n&lt;ExcalidrawSVG src={roleHierarchy} alt=\&quot;Jazz role hierarchy showing admin, manager, writer, writeOnly, and reader roles from highest to lowest privilege\&quot; maxWidth=\&quot;480px\&quot; /&gt;\n\nWhen we create a Group and grant public write access, the permission structure looks like this:\n\n&lt;ExcalidrawSVG src={groupPermissions} alt=\&quot;Jazz Group permissions diagram showing Creator with admin role and everyone with writer role, allowing anyone with the URL to read and write while the creator retains full admin control\&quot; maxWidth=\&quot;520px\&quot; /&gt;\n\nYou might wonder: what stops a malicious user from upgrading their own role from `writer` to `admin`? Jazz enforces permissions cryptographically — not on a server you have to trust, but in the data itself.\n\nEvery change to a CoValue is signed with the author&#39;s private key (Ed25519). When any peer receives a transaction, it verifies the signature and checks whether that account actually had permission to make that change. A writer trying to modify Group roles? The signature is valid, but the Group&#39;s internal rules reject it — only admins can change roles. The transaction gets discarded.\n\n&lt;ExcalidrawSVG src={rolePermissionCheck} alt=\&quot;Flowchart showing how Writer and Admin go through the same validation pipeline — both sign a transaction and pass signature verification, but diverge at the permission check where the Writer is rejected and the Admin is accepted\&quot; maxWidth=\&quot;480px\&quot; /&gt;\n\nThis means even the Jazz Cloud sync server can&#39;t tamper with your data — it just relays signed transactions. If the server modified anything, the signatures wouldn&#39;t match and peers would reject it. Jazz also encrypts data with a shared read key (XSalsa20), so the server can&#39;t even read what it&#39;s relaying.\n\n&lt;Aside type=\&quot;note\&quot;&gt;\nFor more complex apps, Jazz supports granular permissions on nested CoValues. Each nested CoValue can have its own Group with different roles — for example, a project board where managers can edit columns but clients can only read specific tasks. Groups can also be members of other groups, enabling cascading permission hierarchies.\n&lt;/Aside&gt;\n\nWith permissions covered, let&#39;s build something more ambitious.\n\n## What We&#39;re Building: A Real-Time Vue 3 Todo App\n\nA todo list app that:\n\n- Syncs in real-time across tabs and devices via Jazz Cloud\n- Works offline with a toggle to simulate going on/off the network\n- Supports drag-and-drop reordering via `useSortable`\n- Shows a dynamic page title with the count of incomplete todos\n- Generates a shareable URL so anyone with the link sees the same list\n- Includes the Jazz Inspector for debugging CoValues in development\n\nTry it out — both todo apps below are independent Jazz clients, each running as a Vue component embedded in this page. Add a todo in one and watch it sync to the other via Jazz Cloud:\n\n&lt;JazzTodoDemo /&gt;\n\n&lt;Aside type=\&quot;info\&quot;&gt;\nClick the Jazz icon in the bottom-right corner to open the Jazz Inspector. You can copy any `co_z...` CoValue ID shown in the app UI, paste it into the inspector, and hit \&quot;Inspect CoValue\&quot; to see the raw data inside — its fields, current values, and sync status.\n&lt;/Aside&gt;\n\nHere&#39;s the high-level architecture:\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart LR\n    subgraph BrowserA[\&quot;Browser A (Tab 1)\&quot;]\n        AppA[\&quot;Vue App\&quot;] --&gt; IDB_A[\&quot;Local IndexedDB\&quot;]\n    end\n\n    subgraph Cloud[\&quot;Jazz Cloud\&quot;]\n        Sync[\&quot;Sync Server\&quot;]\n        Store[\&quot;Persistent Store\&quot;]\n        Sync &lt;--&gt; Store\n    end\n\n    subgraph BrowserB[\&quot;Browser B (Tab 2)\&quot;]\n        AppB[\&quot;Vue App\&quot;] --&gt; IDB_B[\&quot;Local IndexedDB\&quot;]\n    end\n\n    IDB_A &lt;--&gt;|WebSocket| Sync\n    IDB_B &lt;--&gt;|WebSocket| Sync\n```\n\nLet&#39;s build it step by step.\n\n## Project Setup\n\nYou&#39;ll need Node.js v20+ and a package manager (we&#39;ll use pnpm, but npm/yarn work too).\n\nStart with a fresh Vue project (select TypeScript when prompted) and install the dependencies:\n\n```bash\nnpm create vue@latest vue-jazz-todo\ncd vue-jazz-todo\n\npnpm add jazz-tools community-jazz-vue @vueuse/core @vueuse/integrations sortablejs fractional-indexing tailwindcss @tailwindcss/vite\npnpm add -D @types/sortablejs vite-plugin-vue-devtools\n```\n\nHere&#39;s the project structure we&#39;ll end up with:\n\n&lt;FileTree\n  tree={[\n    {\n      name: \&quot;vue-jazz-todo\&quot;,\n      open: true,\n      children: [\n        {\n          name: \&quot;src\&quot;,\n          open: true,\n          children: [\n            { name: \&quot;main.ts\&quot;, comment: \&quot;App entry point\&quot; },\n            { name: \&quot;App.vue\&quot;, comment: \&quot;JazzVueProvider wrapper\&quot; },\n            { name: \&quot;TodoApp.vue\&quot;, comment: \&quot;Main todo UI\&quot; },\n            { name: \&quot;schema.ts\&quot;, comment: \&quot;Jazz CoValue definitions\&quot; },\n            {\n              name: \&quot;assets\&quot;,\n              open: true,\n              children: [\n                { name: \&quot;main.css\&quot;, comment: \&quot;Tailwind CSS import\&quot; },\n              ],\n            },\n          ],\n        },\n        { name: \&quot;vite.config.ts\&quot;, comment: \&quot;Build config\&quot; },\n        { name: \&quot;index.html\&quot;, comment: \&quot;HTML shell\&quot; },\n        { name: \&quot;package.json\&quot; },\n      ],\n    },\n  ]}\n/&gt;\n\n## Defining the Schema\n\nJazz uses Collaborative Values (CoValues) as its building blocks — reactive, synced data structures. If you&#39;ve used Zod before, the schema API will feel familiar. Create `src/schema.ts`:\n\n```ts\nimport { co, z } from \&quot;jazz-tools\&quot;;\n\nexport const ToDo = co.map({ title: z.string(), completed: z.boolean(), order: z.string() });\nexport const ToDoList = co.list(ToDo);\n```\n\nTwo lines. `co.map` defines a collaborative object with typed fields, `co.list` defines an ordered list. The `order` field stores a fractional index string for drag-and-drop — we&#39;ll cover why in the reordering section. Jazz handles sync, persistence, and conflict resolution under the hood.\n\n&lt;Aside type=\&quot;note\&quot;&gt;\nUnder the hood, Jazz&#39;s CoValues are built on [CRDTs](https://jakelazaroff.com/words/an-interactive-intro-to-crdts/) (Conflict-free Replicated Data Types). Unlike Dexie.js where the server handles conflicts, Jazz bakes conflict resolution directly into the data structures — you never have to think about it.\n&lt;/Aside&gt;\n\nHere&#39;s what that looks like in practice. A `CoMap` tracks every change from every device. When Alice sets `completed: false` at 8:05 AM and Bob sets `completed: true` at 8:03 AM, the later timestamp wins. Step through the timeline to see how the resolved state changes as transactions arrive:\n\n&lt;CoMapVisualizer client:only=\&quot;react\&quot; /&gt;\n\n## Entry Point and Build Configuration\n\nThe entry point is standard Vue. Update `src/main.ts`:\n\n```ts\nimport { createApp } from \&quot;vue\&quot;;\nimport App from \&quot;./App.vue\&quot;;\nimport \&quot;./assets/main.css\&quot;;\n\ncreateApp(App).mount(\&quot;#app\&quot;);\n```\n\nFor Tailwind CSS v4, replace `src/assets/main.css` with a single import, no `tailwind.config.js` needed:\n\n```css\n@import \&quot;tailwindcss\&quot;;\n```\n\nWe also need to tell Vue about the Jazz Inspector custom element so Vue doesn&#39;t try to resolve it as a component. Update `vite.config.ts`:\n\n```ts\nimport { fileURLToPath, URL } from &#39;node:url&#39;\nimport { defineConfig } from &#39;vite&#39;\nimport vue from &#39;@vitejs/plugin-vue&#39;\nimport vueDevTools from &#39;vite-plugin-vue-devtools&#39;\nimport tailwindcss from &#39;@tailwindcss/vite&#39;\n\nexport default defineConfig({\n  plugins: [\n    vue({\n      template: {\n        compilerOptions: {\n          isCustomElement: (tag) =&gt; tag === &#39;jazz-inspector&#39;,\n        },\n      },\n    }),\n    vueDevTools(),\n    tailwindcss(),\n  ],\n  resolve: {\n    alias: {\n      &#39;@&#39;: fileURLToPath(new URL(&#39;./src&#39;, import.meta.url))\n    },\n  },\n})\n```\n\nThe `isCustomElement` line is important — Jazz ships with a built-in inspector for browsing and debugging CoValues at runtime. It appears as a floating panel where you can click into any CoValue to see its current state, history, and sync status. Since the inspector is a Web Component (`&lt;jazz-inspector /&gt;`), we need to tell Vue not to resolve it as a Vue component.\n\n## Setting Up the Jazz Provider\n\nInstead of manually creating a context manager, we use the `JazzVueProvider` component from `community-jazz-vue`. It handles context creation, cleanup, and provides Jazz to all child components via Vue&#39;s dependency injection.\n\nCreate `src/App.vue`:\n\n```vue\n&lt;script setup lang=\&quot;ts\&quot;&gt;\nimport { ref, computed } from \&quot;vue\&quot;;\nimport { JazzVueProvider } from \&quot;community-jazz-vue\&quot;;\nimport \&quot;jazz-tools/inspector/register-custom-element\&quot;;\nimport TodoApp from \&quot;./TodoApp.vue\&quot;;\n\nconst isOnline = ref(true);\nconst syncConfig = computed(() =&gt; ({\n  peer: \&quot;wss://cloud.jazz.tools/?key=vue-jazz-todo-example\&quot; as const,\n  when: isOnline.value ? (\&quot;always\&quot; as const) : (\&quot;never\&quot; as const),\n}));\n&lt;/script&gt;\n\n&lt;template&gt;\n  &lt;JazzVueProvider :sync=\&quot;syncConfig\&quot;&gt;\n    &lt;TodoApp v-model:is-online=\&quot;isOnline\&quot; /&gt;\n    &lt;jazz-inspector /&gt;\n  &lt;/JazzVueProvider&gt;\n&lt;/template&gt;\n```\n\nThree things worth understanding about this setup:\n\n- `JazzVueProvider` wraps the entire app and takes a `sync` prop. It only renders children once the Jazz context is ready, so downstream components can safely assume Jazz is available.\n- The sync config is reactive — the `computed` derives the config from `isOnline`. When the user toggles the switch, `when` flips between `\&quot;always\&quot;` and `\&quot;never\&quot;`, and Jazz switches between syncing and offline mode.\n- `import \&quot;jazz-tools/inspector/register-custom-element\&quot;` registers the `&lt;jazz-inspector&gt;` Web Component as a side-effect import. The `isOnline` state lives here and is passed down via `v-model:is-online`, keeping the sync config and toggle UI separated.\n\n## Building the Todo App\n\nNow for the main component. Create `src/TodoApp.vue` and let&#39;s build it up piece by piece.\n\n### Imports and Setup\n\n```ts\nimport { ref, computed, useTemplateRef, watchEffect } from \&quot;vue\&quot;;\nimport { co, Group } from \&quot;jazz-tools\&quot;;\nimport { useCoState } from \&quot;community-jazz-vue\&quot;;\nimport { useClipboard, useUrlSearchParams, useTitle, useFocus } from \&quot;@vueuse/core\&quot;;\nimport { useSortable, removeNode, insertNodeAt } from \&quot;@vueuse/integrations/useSortable\&quot;;\nimport { generateKeyBetween } from \&quot;fractional-indexing\&quot;;\nimport { ToDo, ToDoList } from \&quot;./schema\&quot;;\n\nconst isOnline = defineModel&lt;boolean&gt;(\&quot;isOnline\&quot;, { required: true });\nconst newTitle = ref(\&quot;\&quot;);\nconst { copy, copied } = useClipboard({ copiedDuring: 2000 });\n```\n\nWe receive `isOnline` from the parent via `defineModel` and set up a ref for the input field plus VueUse&#39;s clipboard composable for the \&quot;Copy link\&quot; button.\n\n### Routing via URL\n\n```ts\nconst params = useUrlSearchParams(\&quot;history\&quot;);\nconst listId = ref&lt;string | undefined&gt;(params.id as string | undefined);\n\nif (!listId.value) {\n  const group = Group.create();\n  group.addMember(\&quot;everyone\&quot;, \&quot;writer\&quot;);\n  const newList = ToDoList.create([], { owner: group });\n  listId.value = newList.$jazz.id;\n  params.id = newList.$jazz.id;\n}\n```\n\nWe use VueUse&#39;s `useUrlSearchParams(\&quot;history\&quot;)` instead of raw `URLSearchParams`. The `\&quot;history\&quot;` mode uses the History API (no page reload) and gives us a reactive object. If the URL already has an `?id=` parameter, we subscribe to that existing list. Otherwise, we create a new list owned by a Group with public write access — the same pattern from the permissions section — so anyone with the link can read and write.\n\n### Subscribing to the List\n\n```ts\nconst todoList = useCoState(ToDoList, listId, {\n  resolve: { $each: true },\n});\n\nconst todos = computed(() =&gt; {\n  const list = todoList.value;\n  if (!list?.$isLoaded) return [];\n  return [...list].sort((a, b) =&gt; (a.order &lt; b.order ? -1 : a.order &gt; b.order ? 1 : 0));\n});\n```\n\n`useCoState` is the core composable from `community-jazz-vue`. It takes a CoValue schema, an ID (which can be a ref), and a resolve query. It returns a Vue `Ref` that starts as unloaded, populates once available, and re-renders on both local and remote changes.\n\nThe `resolve: { $each: true }` tells Jazz to deeply load each item in the list. Without it, you&#39;d get the list but each ToDo entry would be an unresolved reference. Items are sorted by their `order` field rather than their position in the CoList.\n\nIf you&#39;re interested in how Vue composables like this are designed, I wrote about the patterns here:\n\n&lt;InternalLink slug=\&quot;vueuse_composables_style_guide\&quot;&gt;Vue Composables Style Guide: Lessons from VueUse&#39;s Codebase&lt;/InternalLink&gt;\n\n### Dynamic Page Title\n\n```ts\nconst pageTitle = useTitle(\&quot;To Do\&quot;);\nwatchEffect(() =&gt; {\n  const count = todos.value.filter((t) =&gt; !t.completed).length;\n  pageTitle.value = count &gt; 0 ? `(${count}) To Do` : \&quot;To Do\&quot;;\n});\n```\n\nA small UX touch — the browser tab shows \&quot;(3) To Do\&quot; when there are 3 incomplete items.\n\n### CRUD Operations\n\n```ts\nconst inputEl = useTemplateRef&lt;HTMLInputElement&gt;(\&quot;inputEl\&quot;);\nconst { focused: inputFocused } = useFocus(inputEl);\n\nfunction addTodo() {\n  const list = todoList.value;\n  const title = newTitle.value.trim();\n  if (!title || !list?.$isLoaded) return;\n  const sorted = todos.value;\n  const lastOrder = sorted.length &gt; 0 ? sorted[sorted.length - 1]!.order : null;\n  const order = generateKeyBetween(lastOrder, null);\n  list.$jazz.push({ title, completed: false, order });\n  newTitle.value = \&quot;\&quot;;\n  inputFocused.value = true;\n}\n\nfunction toggleTodo(todo: co.loaded&lt;typeof ToDo&gt;) {\n  todo.$jazz.set(\&quot;completed\&quot;, !todo.completed);\n}\n\nfunction deleteTodo(todo: co.loaded&lt;typeof ToDo&gt;) {\n  const list = todoList.value;\n  if (!list?.$isLoaded) return;\n  const listIndex = [...list].findIndex((t) =&gt; t.$jazz.id === todo.$jazz.id);\n  if (listIndex !== -1) list.$jazz.remove(listIndex);\n}\n\nconst copyLink = () =&gt; copy(window.location.href);\n```\n\nEvery loaded CoValue exposes a `$jazz` accessor for mutations — `$jazz.push()`, `$jazz.set()`, `$jazz.remove()`. These mutations are applied locally and synced to all connected peers automatically. No \&quot;save\&quot; button, no API call.\n\n`addTodo` generates a fractional index via `generateKeyBetween(lastOrder, null)`, which creates a key that sorts after all existing items. `deleteTodo` finds the item by its CoValue ID instead of relying on the array index — since our `todos` computed is sorted by `order`, the display index won&#39;t match the `CoList` position.\n\n### The Sync Lifecycle\n\nHere&#39;s what happens when you call a mutation like `list.$jazz.push(...)`:\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart LR\n    A[\&quot;list.$jazz.push(...)\&quot;] --&gt; B[\&quot;Local IndexedDB\&quot;]\n    B --&gt; C[\&quot;Vue re-renders via shallowRef\&quot;]\n    B --&gt; D[\&quot;Jazz Cloud Sync Server\&quot;]\n    D --&gt; E[\&quot;Other Browsers\&quot;]\n    E --&gt; F[\&quot;useCoState() triggers update\&quot;]\n    F --&gt; G[\&quot;Vue re-renders\&quot;]\n```\n\nThe mutation returns immediately — your UI updates before the sync even starts. When the data reaches other peers, their `useCoState` subscriptions fire and Vue re-renders on their end too.\n\n## The TodoApp.vue Template\n\nHere&#39;s the complete template that ties together all the script logic — the add form, the sortable list, the online toggle, and the shareable link:\n\n```vue\n&lt;template&gt;\n  &lt;div class=\&quot;min-h-screen bg-gray-950 flex items-start justify-center pt-16 px-4\&quot;&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;w-full max-w-md\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;!-- Header with online toggle --&gt;\n      &lt;div class=\&quot;flex items-center justify-between mb-8\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;div class=\&quot;flex items-center gap-2\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;svg class=\&quot;w-7 h-7 text-blue-500\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot; fill=\&quot;currentColor\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;path d=\&quot;M12 3v10.55c-.59-.34-1.27-.55-2-.55C7.79 13 6 14.79 6 17s1.79 4 4 4 4-1.79 4-4V7h4V3h-6z\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/svg&gt;\n          &lt;span class=\&quot;text-white text-xl font-semibold tracking-tight\&quot;&gt;jazz&lt;/span&gt;\n        &lt;/div&gt;\n        &lt;div class=\&quot;flex items-center gap-2\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;span class=\&quot;text-gray-300 text-sm\&quot;&gt;Online&lt;/span&gt;\n          &lt;button\n            @click=\&quot;isOnline = !isOnline\&quot;\n            :class=\&quot;[\n              &#39;relative inline-flex h-6 w-11 items-center rounded-full transition-colors&#39;,\n              isOnline ? &#39;bg-blue-600&#39; : &#39;bg-gray-600&#39;,\n            ]\&quot;\n          &gt;\n            &lt;span\n              :class=\&quot;[\n                &#39;inline-block h-4 w-4 rounded-full bg-white transition-transform&#39;,\n                isOnline ? &#39;translate-x-6&#39; : &#39;translate-x-1&#39;,\n              ]\&quot;\n            /&gt;\n          &lt;/button&gt;\n        &lt;/div&gt;\n      &lt;/div&gt;\n\n      &lt;!-- Card --&gt;\n      &lt;div class=\&quot;bg-gray-900 border border-gray-700 rounded-xl p-6\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;h1 class=\&quot;text-3xl font-bold text-white mb-6\&quot;&gt;To Do&lt;/h1&gt;\n\n        &lt;div v-if=\&quot;!todoList?.$isLoaded\&quot; class=\&quot;text-gray-400 text-center py-8\&quot;&gt;\n          Loading...\n        &lt;/div&gt;\n\n        &lt;template v-else&gt;\n          &lt;form @submit.prevent=\&quot;addTodo\&quot; class=\&quot;mb-6 space-y-3\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;input\n              ref=\&quot;inputEl\&quot;\n              v-model=\&quot;newTitle\&quot;\n              placeholder=\&quot;New task\&quot;\n              class=\&quot;w-full px-3 py-2 bg-gray-800 border border-gray-600 rounded-lg text-white placeholder-gray-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-transparent\&quot;\n            /&gt;\n            &lt;button\n              type=\&quot;submit\&quot;\n              class=\&quot;w-full px-4 py-2 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors font-medium\&quot;\n            &gt;\n              Add\n            &lt;/button&gt;\n          &lt;/form&gt;\n\n          &lt;ul ref=\&quot;todoListEl\&quot; class=\&quot;space-y-2\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;li\n              v-for=\&quot;(todo, index) in todos\&quot;\n              :key=\&quot;todo.$jazz.id\&quot;\n              class=\&quot;group flex items-center gap-3 p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-gray-800\&quot;\n            &gt;\n              &lt;span\n                class=\&quot;drag-handle cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing text-gray-600 group-hover:text-gray-400 transition-colors select-none\&quot;\n                title=\&quot;Drag to reorder\&quot;\n              &gt;\n                &lt;svg class=\&quot;w-4 h-4\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot; fill=\&quot;currentColor\&quot;&gt;\n                  &lt;circle cx=\&quot;9\&quot; cy=\&quot;6\&quot; r=\&quot;1.5\&quot; /&gt;&lt;circle cx=\&quot;15\&quot; cy=\&quot;6\&quot; r=\&quot;1.5\&quot; /&gt;\n                  &lt;circle cx=\&quot;9\&quot; cy=\&quot;12\&quot; r=\&quot;1.5\&quot; /&gt;&lt;circle cx=\&quot;15\&quot; cy=\&quot;12\&quot; r=\&quot;1.5\&quot; /&gt;\n                  &lt;circle cx=\&quot;9\&quot; cy=\&quot;18\&quot; r=\&quot;1.5\&quot; /&gt;&lt;circle cx=\&quot;15\&quot; cy=\&quot;18\&quot; r=\&quot;1.5\&quot; /&gt;\n                &lt;/svg&gt;\n              &lt;/span&gt;\n              &lt;input\n                type=\&quot;checkbox\&quot;\n                :checked=\&quot;todo.completed\&quot;\n                @change=\&quot;toggleTodo(todo)\&quot;\n                class=\&quot;h-4 w-4 rounded border-gray-600 bg-gray-800 text-blue-600 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:ring-offset-gray-900\&quot;\n              /&gt;\n              &lt;span\n                class=\&quot;flex-1\&quot;\n                :class=\&quot;todo.completed ? &#39;line-through text-gray-500&#39; : &#39;text-gray-200&#39;\&quot;\n              &gt;\n                {{ todo.title }}\n              &lt;/span&gt;\n              &lt;button\n                @click=\&quot;deleteTodo(todo)\&quot;\n                class=\&quot;opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-gray-500 hover:text-red-400 p-1\&quot;\n                title=\&quot;Delete\&quot;\n              &gt;\n                &lt;svg class=\&quot;w-4 h-4\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot; fill=\&quot;none\&quot; stroke=\&quot;currentColor\&quot; stroke-width=\&quot;2\&quot;&gt;\n                  &lt;path d=\&quot;M18 6L6 18M6 6l12 12\&quot; /&gt;\n                &lt;/svg&gt;\n              &lt;/button&gt;\n            &lt;/li&gt;\n          &lt;/ul&gt;\n\n          &lt;p v-if=\&quot;todos.length === 0\&quot; class=\&quot;text-gray-500 text-center py-4\&quot;&gt;\n            No todos yet. Add one above!\n          &lt;/p&gt;\n\n          &lt;div v-if=\&quot;listId\&quot; class=\&quot;mt-6 flex items-center gap-2\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;p class=\&quot;text-xs text-gray-500 break-all flex-1\&quot;&gt;\n              List ID: {{ listId }}\n            &lt;/p&gt;\n            &lt;button\n              @click=\&quot;copyLink\&quot;\n              class=\&quot;shrink-0 px-3 py-1 text-xs rounded-md border transition-colors\&quot;\n              :class=\&quot;copied\n                ? &#39;border-green-600 text-green-400&#39;\n                : &#39;border-gray-600 text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-200 hover:border-gray-500&#39;\&quot;\n            &gt;\n              {{ copied ? \&quot;Copied!\&quot; : \&quot;Copy link\&quot; }}\n            &lt;/button&gt;\n          &lt;/div&gt;\n        &lt;/template&gt;\n      &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n  &lt;/div&gt;\n&lt;/template&gt;\n```\n\nIn the template, `:key=\&quot;todo.$jazz.id\&quot;` gives Vue a stable, globally unique key for each item. The `ref=\&quot;inputEl\&quot;` connects to `useFocus` so the input regains focus after adding a todo. And `@change=\&quot;toggleTodo(todo)\&quot;` shows how clean mutations are — no actions, no dispatching, no reducers.\n\n## Drag-and-Drop Reordering\n\nWe use [`useSortable`](https://vueuse.org/integrations/useSortable/) from VueUse for drag-and-drop. The simplest approach would be to call `splice` on the `CoList` directly — remove the item from its old position, insert it at the new one. For a single user, that works fine.\n\n### The Problem with `splice`\n\nJazz&#39;s `CoList` implements `splice` as a delete-plus-insert, not as an atomic move. That distinction matters as soon as two users are involved. If both users reorder the same item while offline, each one generates an independent delete-plus-insert. When they sync back up, the list CRDT sees two separate insert operations — and the item appears twice.\n\nThis is a fundamental issue with list CRDTs: there&#39;s no \&quot;move\&quot; operation, only deletes and inserts. So we need a different strategy for ordering.\n\n### Fractional Indexing to the Rescue\n\n[Fractional indexing](https://www.npmjs.com/package/fractional-indexing) (by Rocicorp, based on [this Observable post](https://observablehq.com/@dgreensp/implementing-fractional-indexing) by David Greenspan) sidesteps the problem entirely. Instead of moving an item in the list, you store an `order` field on each item and update only that field when reordering. When you move an item between positions A and C, `generateKeyBetween(\&quot;a\&quot;, \&quot;c\&quot;)` returns a key like `\&quot;b\&quot;` that sorts between them. The rest of the list stays untouched.\n\n&lt;FractionalIndexingVisualizer client:only=\&quot;react\&quot; /&gt;\n\nBecause `order` is a field on a `CoMap`, updates use last-writer-wins semantics. The worst case during a concurrent edit is that one user&#39;s reorder \&quot;wins\&quot; — but the item never duplicates.\n\n### Implementation\n\nHere&#39;s how it looks with `useSortable`:\n\n```ts\nconst todoListEl = useTemplateRef&lt;HTMLElement&gt;(\&quot;todoListEl\&quot;);\n\nuseSortable(todoListEl, todos, {\n  handle: \&quot;.drag-handle\&quot;,\n  animation: 150,\n  onUpdate: (e) =&gt; {\n    // Revert SortableJS DOM manipulation — let Vue re-render from data\n    removeNode(e.item);\n    insertNodeAt(e.from, e.item, e.oldIndex!);\n\n    const list = todoList.value;\n    if (!list?.$isLoaded || e.oldIndex == null || e.newIndex == null) return;\n\n    const sorted = todos.value;\n    const before = sorted[e.newIndex - 1]?.order ?? null;\n    const after = sorted[e.newIndex + (e.newIndex &gt; e.oldIndex ? 1 : 0)]?.order ?? null;\n    const item = sorted[e.oldIndex];\n    if (item) item.$jazz.set(\&quot;order\&quot;, generateKeyBetween(before, after));\n  },\n});\n```\n\nThe `onUpdate` handler contains a subtle DOM revert pattern: SortableJS directly manipulates the DOM when the user drags an item, but our source of truth is the `order` field on each `CoMap`. So we first undo the DOM change, then update the `order` field. Vue&#39;s computed re-sorts and re-renders correctly.\n\nThe reorder syncs to all peers just like any other mutation. If you&#39;ve worked with cross-tab state syncing before, you&#39;ll know how tricky this can be:\n\n&lt;InternalLink slug=\&quot;building-pinia-plugin-cross-tab-sync\&quot;&gt;Building a Pinia Plugin for Cross-Tab State Syncing&lt;/InternalLink&gt;\n\n## Running It\n\n```bash\npnpm dev\n```\n\nOpen two browser tabs. Add a todo in one, watch it appear instantly in the other. Toggle \&quot;Online\&quot; off, add more todos, toggle back on — they sync up. Copy the link, open it in an incognito window — same list.\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe full project is four files of application code:\n\n- `src/schema.ts` (4 lines) — CoValue definitions\n- `src/App.vue` (20 lines) — Provider + inspector + online toggle\n- `src/TodoApp.vue` (~80 lines script + ~125 lines template) — The complete app\n- `vite.config.ts` (26 lines) — Build config with custom element support\n\nWhat surprised me most coming from the Dexie.js approach is how little code you need. Jazz eliminates the entire backend-sync-API stack. You define your data, mutate it locally, and it syncs.\n\nTwo things worth highlighting: fractional indexing for drag-and-drop avoids the duplicate-item problem that `CoList` splice-based reordering can cause during concurrent offline edits. And Jazz Groups with `addMember(\&quot;everyone\&quot;, \&quot;writer\&quot;)` make the shared URL actually accessible — without this, CoValues are private to the creator.\n\nCheck out the [Jazz documentation](https://jazz.tools) for more, and the [community-jazz-vue package](https://www.npmjs.com/package/community-jazz-vue) ([source code](https://github.com/garden-co/jazz/tree/main/packages/community-jazz-vue/src)) for the full Vue API.\n\n---\n\n**Source code:** [github.com/alexanderop/vue-jazz-todo-example](https://github.com/alexanderop/vue-jazz-todo-example)&quot;]}" ssr client="load" opts="{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;PostCopyButton&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:true}" await-children><button class="focus-outline inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 rounded-md border border-skin-line bg-skin-card px-2.5 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium text-skin-base opacity-80 transition-all hover:border-skin-accent/50 hover:text-skin-accent hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Copy post as markdown" title="Copy post as markdown for AI/LLM"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="h-3.5 w-3.5" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor"><path d="M8 3a1 1 0 011-1h2a1 1 0 110 2H9a1 1 0 01-1-1z"></path><path d="M6 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2V5a2 2 0 00-2-2 3 3 0 01-3 3H9a3 3 0 01-3-3z"></path></svg><span>Copy Post</span></button><!--astro:end--></astro-island> </div> <nav class="mb-8 astro-sbmhws2g" aria-labelledby="series-heading"> <div class="mb-1 text-sm font-bold tracking-wide text-skin-accent astro-sbmhws2g"> Local-First Web Development Series </div> <h2 id="series-heading" class="mb-2 text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-widest text-skin-accent astro-sbmhws2g">

Learn how to create offline-capable, installable web apps using Vite and modern PWA techniques. </div> </li><li class="relative flex flex-col rounded py-2 pl-4 transition-all   astro-sbmhws2g"> <div class="flex items-center gap-2 astro-sbmhws2g"> <span class="font-mono text-xs text-skin-base/60 astro-sbmhws2g"> 3.
</span> <a href="/posts/sqlite-vue3-offline-first-web-apps-guide/" class="font-medium underline-offset-4 text-skin-accent/80 hover:underline astro-sbmhws2g"> SQLite in Vue: Complete Guide to Building Offline-First Web Apps </a>  </div> <div class="ml-6 mt-1 text-xs text-skin-base/70 astro-sbmhws2g"> Learn how to build offline-capable Vue 3 apps using SQLite and WebAssembly in 2024. Step-by-step tutorial includes code examples for database operations, query playground implementation, and best practices for offline-first applications. </div> </li><li class="relative flex flex-col rounded py-2 pl-4 transition-all   astro-sbmhws2g"> <div class="flex items-center gap-2 astro-sbmhws2g"> <span class="font-mono text-xs text-skin-base/60 astro-sbmhws2g"> 4.
</span> <a href="/posts/building-local-first-apps-vue-dexie/" class="font-medium underline-offset-4 text-skin-accent/80 hover:underline astro-sbmhws2g"> Building Local-First Apps with Vue and Dexie.js </a>  </div> <div class="ml-6 mt-1 text-xs text-skin-base/70 astro-sbmhws2g"> Learn how to create offline-capable, local-first applications using Vue 3 and Dexie.js. Discover patterns for data persistence, synchronization, and optimal user experience. </div> </li><li class="relative flex flex-col rounded py-2 pl-4 transition-all border-l-4 border-skin-accent bg-skin-card/60  astro-sbmhws2g"> <div class="flex items-center gap-2 astro-sbmhws2g"> <span class="font-mono text-xs text-skin-accent astro-sbmhws2g"> 5.
</span> <a href="/posts/building-real-time-todo-app-jazz-vue/" class="font-medium underline-offset-4 pointer-events-none text-skin-accent astro-sbmhws2g" aria-current="page"> Building a Real-Time Todo App with Jazz and Vue 3 </a> <span class="ml-2 text-xs font-bold text-green-400 astro-sbmhws2g">
(current)
</span> </div> <div class="ml-6 mt-1 text-xs text-skin-base/70 astro-sbmhws2g"> Build a real-time, offline-capable todo app with Jazz and Vue 3. Learn CoValues, drag-and-drop with fractional indexing, and shareable URLs — no backend needed. </div> </li>  </ol> <div class="mt-4 border-b border-skin-line opacity-40 astro-sbmhws2g"></div> </nav>  <article id="article" class="prose mx-auto mt-8 max-w-5xl astro-vj4tpspi"> <h2 id="tldr">TLDR<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#tldr"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h2>
<p>Build a real-time, offline-capable todo app with Jazz and Vue 3. Jazz replaces your entire backend with collaborative data structures called CoValues. Combined with <code>community-jazz-vue</code>, you get composables like <code>useCoState</code> that plug into Vue’s reactivity system. The app syncs across tabs and devices, supports drag-and-drop with fractional indexing, and generates shareable URLs.</p>
<h2 id="why-jazz-replaces-your-entire-backend">Why Jazz Replaces Your Entire Backend<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#why-jazz-replaces-your-entire-backend"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h2>
<p>You want real-time collaboration, offline support, and shareable URLs. In a traditional stack, that means building a sync server, a conflict resolution strategy, a permissions layer, and an API. Jazz collapses all of that into collaborative data structures called CoValues.</p>
<p>Think of Vue’s <code>ref</code> — it keeps the virtual DOM in sync with the real DOM. CoValues take that further: they sync your data across devices, across users, and across network boundaries. You mutate data locally, Jazz handles the rest.</p>
<figure class="excalidraw-figure astro-hxyrieg5" style="max-width: 520px; margin-inline: auto;"> <div class="excalidraw-svg astro-hxyrieg5" role="img" aria-label="CoValue overview showing how you mutate locally and Jazz automatically handles sync via real-time CRDT merge, persistence via IndexedDB with offline-first support, and security via Groups, roles, and E2E encryption"><svg version="1.1" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 580 340" width="100%" class="excalidraw-rendered" preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet">

<p>This is the next post in my local-first series, and it covers how to build a complete Vue 3 app on top of Jazz. You can find the official Jazz documentation at <a href="https://jazz.tools/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">jazz.tools</a>.</p>
<p>Combined with <code>community-jazz-vue</code>, a community-maintained Vue binding, you get composables like <code>useCoState</code> and a provider component that plug directly into Vue’s reactivity system.</p>
<p>If you’re new to local-first, start with the first post in this series:</p>
<span class="internal-link-wrapper astro-3tyn5ojg"> <a href="/posts/what-is-local-first-web-development/" class="internal-link astro-3tyn5ojg"> What is Local-first Web Development? </a> <span class="preview-card astro-3tyn5ojg" role="tooltip"> <span class="preview-content astro-3tyn5ojg"> <span class="preview-title astro-3tyn5ojg">What is Local-first Web Development?</span> <span class="preview-description astro-3tyn5ojg">What is local-first software and why does it matter? This guide covers local-first architecture, offline-capable apps with automatic sync, data ownership, and how to build a local-first web app with Vue step by step.</span> <span class="preview-tags astro-3tyn5ojg"> <span class="preview-tag astro-3tyn5ojg">local-first</span><span class="preview-tag astro-3tyn5ojg">architecture</span><span class="preview-tag astro-3tyn5ojg">vue</span> <span class="preview-tag-more astro-3tyn5ojg">+1</span> </span> <time class="preview-date astro-3tyn5ojg">May 29, 2024</time> </span> </span> </span>  <script>
  function initInternalLinks() {
    const wrappers = document.querySelectorAll(".internal-link-wrapper");

    wrappers.forEach(wrapper => {
      const card = wrapper.querySelector(".preview-card");
      const link = wrapper.querySelector(".internal-link");
      if (!card || !link) return;

      // Skip if already initialized
      if (wrapper.dataset.initialized === "true") return;
      wrapper.dataset.initialized = "true";

      // Function to hide the card
      const hideCard = () => {
        card.classList.remove("is-fixed");
        card.style.removeProperty("--pc-top");
        card.style.removeProperty("--pc-left");
        card.style.opacity = "";
        card.style.visibility = "";
        // Remove scroll listener when hiding
        window.removeEventListener("scroll", hideCard);
      };

      wrapper.addEventListener("mouseenter", () => {
        // Make visible first so it has size
        card.style.opacity = "1";
        card.style.visibility = "visible";

        // Use fixed positioning to escape overflow clipping
        const linkRect = link.getBoundingClientRect();
        const cardRect = card.getBoundingClientRect();

        // Position above by default; flip below if too close to top
        const aboveTop = linkRect.top - 8 - cardRect.height;
        const belowTop = linkRect.bottom + 8;
        const top = aboveTop < 10 ? belowTop : aboveTop;

        // Center horizontally on the link
        const left = linkRect.left + linkRect.width / 2 - cardRect.width / 2;

        // Constrain to viewport
        const vw = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
        const safeLeft = Math.max(8, Math.min(left, vw - cardRect.width - 8));

        // Apply fixed position with coordinates
        card.classList.add("is-fixed");
        card.style.setProperty("--pc-top", `${Math.round(top)}px`);
        card.style.setProperty("--pc-left", `${Math.round(safeLeft)}px`);

        // Hide card on scroll
        window.addEventListener("scroll", hideCard, { passive: true });
      });

      wrapper.addEventListener("mouseleave", hideCard);
    });
  }

  // Initialize on both initial load and after client-side navigation
  document.addEventListener("astro:page-load", initInternalLinks);
</script>
<p>For comparison, here’s the same app built with Dexie.js and IndexedDB:</p>

Discover patterns for data persistence, synchronization, and optimal user experience.</span> <span class="preview-tags astro-3tyn5ojg"> <span class="preview-tag astro-3tyn5ojg">vue</span><span class="preview-tag astro-3tyn5ojg">dexie</span><span class="preview-tag astro-3tyn5ojg">indexeddb</span> <span class="preview-tag-more astro-3tyn5ojg">+1</span> </span> <time class="preview-date astro-3tyn5ojg">Jan 18, 2025</time> </span> </span> </span>  <script>
  function initInternalLinks() {
    const wrappers = document.querySelectorAll(".internal-link-wrapper");

    wrappers.forEach(wrapper => {
      const card = wrapper.querySelector(".preview-card");
      const link = wrapper.querySelector(".internal-link");
      if (!card || !link) return;

      // Skip if already initialized
      if (wrapper.dataset.initialized === "true") return;
      wrapper.dataset.initialized = "true";

      // Function to hide the card
      const hideCard = () => {
        card.classList.remove("is-fixed");
        card.style.removeProperty("--pc-top");
        card.style.removeProperty("--pc-left");
        card.style.opacity = "";
        card.style.visibility = "";
        // Remove scroll listener when hiding
        window.removeEventListener("scroll", hideCard);
      };

      wrapper.addEventListener("mouseenter", () => {
        // Make visible first so it has size
        card.style.opacity = "1";
        card.style.visibility = "visible";

        // Use fixed positioning to escape overflow clipping
        const linkRect = link.getBoundingClientRect();
        const cardRect = card.getBoundingClientRect();

        // Position above by default; flip below if too close to top
        const aboveTop = linkRect.top - 8 - cardRect.height;
        const belowTop = linkRect.bottom + 8;
        const top = aboveTop < 10 ? belowTop : aboveTop;

        // Center horizontally on the link
        const left = linkRect.left + linkRect.width / 2 - cardRect.width / 2;

        // Constrain to viewport
        const vw = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
        const safeLeft = Math.max(8, Math.min(left, vw - cardRect.width - 8));

        // Apply fixed position with coordinates
        card.classList.add("is-fixed");
        card.style.setProperty("--pc-top", `${Math.round(top)}px`);
        card.style.setProperty("--pc-left", `${Math.round(safeLeft)}px`);

        // Hide card on scroll
        window.addEventListener("scroll", hideCard, { passive: true });
      });

      wrapper.addEventListener("mouseleave", hideCard);
    });
  }

  // Initialize on both initial load and after client-side navigation
  document.addEventListener("astro:page-load", initInternalLinks);
</script>

<h2 id="your-first-covalue-a-synced-counter">Your First CoValue: A Synced Counter<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#your-first-covalue-a-synced-counter"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h2>
<p>Vue’s <code>ref</code> keeps the virtual DOM in sync with the real DOM — you update a <code>ref</code>, Vue re-renders. That’s reactive state within one browser tab. Jazz’s <code>useCoState</code> takes that same idea a step further: it keeps your data in sync across devices, across users, and across network boundaries. You mutate locally, Jazz propagates the change to every connected peer.</p>
<p>The simplest CoValue is a single field:</p>
<pre class="astro-code tokyo-night" style="background-color:#1a1b26;color:#a9b1d6;overflow-x:auto;white-space:pre-wrap;word-wrap:break-word" tabindex="0" data-language="ts"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> { </span><span style="color:#0DB9D7">co</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">,</span><span style="color:#0DB9D7"> z</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> }</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> from</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">jazz-tools</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#9D7CD8;font-style:italic">const</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> Counter</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> =</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5"> co</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">.</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7">map</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">({</span><span style="color:#73DACA"> count</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">:</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5"> z</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">.</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7">number</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">()</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> })</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span></code><button type="button" class="copy" data-code="import { co, z } from &#34;jazz-tools&#34;;

const Counter = co.map({ count: z.number() });" onclick="
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.dataset.code);
            this.classList.add('copied');
            setTimeout(() => this.classList.remove('copied'), 3000);
          " aria-label="Copy code"><span class="ready"></span><span class="success"></span></button></pre>
<p>That’s one line of schema. Now subscribe to it in a Vue component:</p>
<pre class="astro-code tokyo-night" style="background-color:#1a1b26;color:#a9b1d6;overflow-x:auto;white-space:pre-wrap;word-wrap:break-word" tabindex="0" data-language="vue"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#BA3C97">&lt;</span><span style="color:#F7768E">script</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> setup</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> lang</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">=</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">ts</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> { </span><span style="color:#0DB9D7">useCoState</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> }</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> from</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">community-jazz-vue</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> { </span><span style="color:#0DB9D7">Counter</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> }</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> from</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">./schema</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#51597D;font-style:italic">// Create a counter and grab its ID</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#BA3C97">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#F7768E">script</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#BA3C97">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#F7768E">p</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&gt;</span><span style="color:#9AA5CE">{{ counter.count }}</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#F7768E">p</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#BA3C97">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#F7768E">button</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> @click</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">=</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">increment</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&gt;</span><span style="color:#9AA5CE">+</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#F7768E">button</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#BA3C97">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#F7768E">div</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#BA3C97">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#F7768E">template</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&gt;</span></span></code><button type="button" class="copy" data-code="<script setup lang=&#34;ts&#34;>
import { ref } from &#34;vue&#34;;
import { useCoState } from &#34;community-jazz-vue&#34;;
import { Counter } from &#34;./schema&#34;;

// Create a counter and grab its ID
const counterId = ref<string | undefined>();
const newCounter = Counter.create({ count: 0 });
counterId.value = newCounter.$jazz.id;

// Subscribe — returns a reactive ref that updates on local and remote changes
const counter = useCoState(Counter, counterId);

function increment() {
  if (counter.value?.$isLoaded) {
    counter.value.$jazz.set(&#34;count&#34;, (counter.value.count ?? 0) + 1);
  }
}

function decrement() {
  if (counter.value?.$isLoaded) {
    counter.value.$jazz.set(&#34;count&#34;, Math.max(0, (counter.value.count ?? 0) - 1));
  }
}
</script>

<template>
  <div v-if=&#34;!counter?.$isLoaded&#34;>Loading...</div>
  <div v-else>
    <p>{{ counter.count }}</p>
    <button @click=&#34;decrement&#34;>−</button>
    <button @click=&#34;increment&#34;>+</button>
  </div>
</template>" onclick="
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.dataset.code);
            this.classList.add('copied');
            setTimeout(() => this.classList.remove('copied'), 3000);
          " aria-label="Copy code"><span class="ready"></span><span class="success"></span></button></pre>
<p>Three things are happening here:</p>
<ol>
<li><code>Counter.create({ count: 0 })</code> creates a new CoValue instance and persists it locally.</li>
<li><code>useCoState(Counter, counterId)</code> subscribes to that CoValue. It returns a reactive <code>Ref</code> that starts unloaded, populates once available, and re-renders on every change — just like Vue’s <code>ref</code>, but across the network.</li>
<li><code>$jazz.set(&quot;count&quot;, ...)</code> mutates the CoValue directly. No API call, no action dispatch — Jazz syncs the change to all connected peers.</li>
</ol>
<p>This already works for a single user. But there’s a problem: <strong>by default, CoValues are private</strong>. Only the creator can read or write them. If you shared this counter’s ID with another user, they’d get nothing — the CoValue is invisible to them.</p>
<h3 id="making-it-shareable-with-groups">Making It Shareable with Groups<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#making-it-shareable-with-groups"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h3>
<p>To let others access the counter, you need a <strong>Group</strong>. Groups are how Jazz controls who gets access and what they can do. Every CoValue has an owner — either an Account (private) or a Group (shared).</p>
<pre class="astro-code tokyo-night" style="background-color:#1a1b26;color:#a9b1d6;overflow-x:auto;white-space:pre-wrap;word-wrap:break-word" tabindex="0" data-language="ts"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> { </span><span style="color:#0DB9D7">Group</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> }</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> from</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">jazz-tools</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#9D7CD8;font-style:italic">const</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> group</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> =</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5"> Group</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">.</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7">create</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">()</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C0CAF5">group</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">.</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7">addMember</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">(</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">everyone</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">,</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">writer</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">)</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#9D7CD8;font-style:italic">const</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> newCounter</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> =</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5"> Counter</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">.</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7">create</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">({</span><span style="color:#73DACA"> count</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">:</span><span style="color:#FF9E64"> 0</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> }</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">,</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> {</span><span style="color:#73DACA"> owner</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">:</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5"> group</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> })</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span></code><button type="button" class="copy" data-code="import { Group } from &#34;jazz-tools&#34;;

const group = Group.create();
group.addMember(&#34;everyone&#34;, &#34;writer&#34;);
const newCounter = Counter.create({ count: 0 }, { owner: group });" onclick="
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.dataset.code);
            this.classList.add('copied');
            setTimeout(() => this.classList.remove('copied'), 3000);
          " aria-label="Copy code"><span class="ready"></span><span class="success"></span></button></pre>
<p>That’s three lines. <code>Group.create()</code> makes a new permission group. <code>addMember(&quot;everyone&quot;, &quot;writer&quot;)</code> grants public write access — the <code>&quot;everyone&quot;</code> keyword is a special shorthand that includes all users, even anonymous guests. Passing <code>{ owner: group }</code> to <code>Counter.create</code> assigns the counter to that group instead of the default private account.</p>
<p>Now anyone who knows the CoValue ID can read and write the same counter. No API keys, no auth server — sharing the ID is all it takes.</p>
<p>Try it — click the + button in one panel and watch the count update in the other. Both panels are independent Jazz clients syncing via Jazz Cloud:</p>

<aside aria-label="Info" class="aside aside-info astro-37uy2q7c"> <div class="aside-content astro-37uy2q7c"> <p class="aside-title astro-37uy2q7c"> <span class="aside-emoji astro-37uy2q7c" role="img" aria-hidden="true">ℹ️</span> Info </p> <section class="aside-body astro-37uy2q7c"> <p>The <code>&quot;everyone&quot;</code> + <code>&quot;writer&quot;</code> combination is intentionally permissive — great for demos and public collaboration. For real apps, Jazz supports granular roles (<code>reader</code>, <code>writer</code>, <code>admin</code>) and per-user membership. We’ll use the same pattern for the todo app below.</p> </section> </div> </aside> 
<p>That’s the entire model: define your data with <code>co.map</code>, subscribe with <code>useCoState</code>, mutate directly. But we glossed over something important — how does Jazz decide who can access a CoValue, and what stops someone from escalating their own permissions?</p>
<h2 id="how-jazz-permissions-work">How Jazz Permissions Work<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#how-jazz-permissions-work"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h2>
<p>The counter example used <code>addMember(&quot;everyone&quot;, &quot;writer&quot;)</code> to make data publicly accessible. Let’s look at what’s happening under the hood.</p>
<p>Jazz defines a role hierarchy where each role includes the permissions of the roles below it:</p>
<figure class="excalidraw-figure astro-hxyrieg5" style="max-width: 480px; margin-inline: auto;"> <div class="excalidraw-svg astro-hxyrieg5" role="img" aria-label="Jazz role hierarchy showing admin, manager, writer, writeOnly, and reader roles from highest to lowest privilege"><svg version="1.1" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 540 520" width="100%" class="excalidraw-rendered" preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet">

<p>When we create a Group and grant public write access, the permission structure looks like this:</p>

<p>You might wonder: what stops a malicious user from upgrading their own role from <code>writer</code> to <code>admin</code>? Jazz enforces permissions cryptographically — not on a server you have to trust, but in the data itself.</p>
<p>Every change to a CoValue is signed with the author’s private key (Ed25519). When any peer receives a transaction, it verifies the signature and checks whether that account actually had permission to make that change. A writer trying to modify Group roles? The signature is valid, but the Group’s internal rules reject it — only admins can change roles. The transaction gets discarded.</p>
<figure class="excalidraw-figure astro-hxyrieg5" style="max-width: 480px; margin-inline: auto;"> <div class="excalidraw-svg astro-hxyrieg5" role="img" aria-label="Flowchart showing how Writer and Admin go through the same validation pipeline — both sign a transaction and pass signature verification, but diverge at the permission check where the Writer is rejected and the Admin is accepted"><svg version="1.1" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 700 730" width="100%" class="excalidraw-rendered" preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet">
  <!-- svg-source:excalidraw -->

rotate(0 35 50)"><path d="M63 73.24 C63.14 79.22, 64.46 82.12, 69.14 101.64 M61.5 72.54 C64.24 79.47, 65.61 85.31, 69.35 102" stroke-width="2" fill="none" class="ed-accent-stroke"></path></g></g></svg></div>  </figure>  
<p>This means even the Jazz Cloud sync server can’t tamper with your data — it just relays signed transactions. If the server modified anything, the signatures wouldn’t match and peers would reject it. Jazz also encrypts data with a shared read key (XSalsa20), so the server can’t even read what it’s relaying.</p>
<aside aria-label="Note" class="aside aside-note astro-37uy2q7c"> <div class="aside-content astro-37uy2q7c"> <p class="aside-title astro-37uy2q7c"> <span class="aside-emoji astro-37uy2q7c" role="img" aria-hidden="true">📝</span> Note </p> <section class="aside-body astro-37uy2q7c"> <p>For more complex apps, Jazz supports granular permissions on nested CoValues. Each nested CoValue can have its own Group with different roles — for example, a project board where managers can edit columns but clients can only read specific tasks. Groups can also be members of other groups, enabling cascading permission hierarchies.</p> </section> </div> </aside> 
<p>With permissions covered, let’s build something more ambitious.</p>
<h2 id="what-were-building-a-real-time-vue-3-todo-app">What We’re Building: A Real-Time Vue 3 Todo App<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#what-were-building-a-real-time-vue-3-todo-app"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h2>
<p>A todo list app that:</p>
<ul>
<li>Syncs in real-time across tabs and devices via Jazz Cloud</li>
<li>Works offline with a toggle to simulate going on/off the network</li>
<li>Supports drag-and-drop reordering via <code>useSortable</code></li>
<li>Shows a dynamic page title with the count of incomplete todos</li>
<li>Generates a shareable URL so anyone with the link sees the same list</li>
<li>Includes the Jazz Inspector for debugging CoValues in development</li>
</ul>
<p>Try it out — both todo apps below are independent Jazz clients, each running as a Vue component embedded in this page. Add a todo in one and watch it sync to the other via Jazz Cloud:</p>
<div class="jazz-todo-demo astro-s2kjw5ml"> <astro-island uid="Z2c4TSR" component-url="/_astro/JazzTodoApp.v9C0Mcxt.js" component-export="default" renderer-url="/_astro/client.Bq2QAC-i.js" props="{&quot;role&quot;:[0,&quot;primary&quot;],&quot;class&quot;:[0,&quot;astro-s2kjw5ml&quot;]}" ssr client="only" opts="{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;JazzTodoApp&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:&quot;vue&quot;}"></astro-island> <astro-island uid="1Qhepd" component-url="/_astro/JazzTodoApp.v9C0Mcxt.js" component-export="default" renderer-url="/_astro/client.Bq2QAC-i.js" props="{&quot;role&quot;:[0,&quot;secondary&quot;],&quot;class&quot;:[0,&quot;astro-s2kjw5ml&quot;]}" ssr client="only" opts="{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;JazzTodoApp&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:&quot;vue&quot;}"></astro-island> </div> <astro-island uid="Z158i9p" component-url="/_astro/JazzInspector.C04_7_4v.js" component-export="default" renderer-url="/_astro/client.Bq2QAC-i.js" props="{&quot;class&quot;:[0,&quot;astro-s2kjw5ml&quot;]}" ssr client="only" opts="{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;JazzInspector&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:&quot;vue&quot;}"></astro-island> 
<aside aria-label="Info" class="aside aside-info astro-37uy2q7c"> <div class="aside-content astro-37uy2q7c"> <p class="aside-title astro-37uy2q7c"> <span class="aside-emoji astro-37uy2q7c" role="img" aria-hidden="true">ℹ️</span> Info </p> <section class="aside-body astro-37uy2q7c"> <p>Click the Jazz icon in the bottom-right corner to open the Jazz Inspector. You can copy any <code>co_z...</code> CoValue ID shown in the app UI, paste it into the inspector, and hit “Inspect CoValue” to see the raw data inside — its fields, current values, and sync status.</p> </section> </div> </aside> 
<p>Here’s the high-level architecture:</p>

<p>Let’s build it step by step.</p>
<h2 id="project-setup">Project Setup<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#project-setup"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h2>
<p>You’ll need Node.js v20+ and a package manager (we’ll use pnpm, but npm/yarn work too).</p>
<p>Start with a fresh Vue project (select TypeScript when prompted) and install the dependencies:</p>

<h2 id="defining-the-schema">Defining the Schema<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#defining-the-schema"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h2>
<p>Jazz uses Collaborative Values (CoValues) as its building blocks — reactive, synced data structures. If you’ve used Zod before, the schema API will feel familiar. Create <code>src/schema.ts</code>:</p>
<pre class="astro-code tokyo-night" style="background-color:#1a1b26;color:#a9b1d6;overflow-x:auto;white-space:pre-wrap;word-wrap:break-word" tabindex="0" data-language="ts"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> { </span><span style="color:#0DB9D7">co</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">,</span><span style="color:#0DB9D7"> z</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> }</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> from</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">jazz-tools</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">export</span><span style="color:#9D7CD8;font-style:italic"> const</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> ToDo</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> =</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5"> co</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">.</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7">map</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">({</span><span style="color:#73DACA"> title</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">:</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5"> z</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">.</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7">string</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">()</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">,</span><span style="color:#73DACA"> completed</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">:</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5"> z</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">.</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7">boolean</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">()</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">,</span><span style="color:#73DACA"> order</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">:</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5"> z</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">.</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7">string</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">()</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> })</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">export</span><span style="color:#9D7CD8;font-style:italic"> const</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> ToDoList</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> =</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5"> co</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">.</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7">list</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">(</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5">ToDo</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">)</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span></code><button type="button" class="copy" data-code="import { co, z } from &#34;jazz-tools&#34;;

export const ToDo = co.map({ title: z.string(), completed: z.boolean(), order: z.string() });
export const ToDoList = co.list(ToDo);" onclick="
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.dataset.code);
            this.classList.add('copied');
            setTimeout(() => this.classList.remove('copied'), 3000);
          " aria-label="Copy code"><span class="ready"></span><span class="success"></span></button></pre>
<p>Two lines. <code>co.map</code> defines a collaborative object with typed fields, <code>co.list</code> defines an ordered list. The <code>order</code> field stores a fractional index string for drag-and-drop — we’ll cover why in the reordering section. Jazz handles sync, persistence, and conflict resolution under the hood.</p>
<aside aria-label="Note" class="aside aside-note astro-37uy2q7c"> <div class="aside-content astro-37uy2q7c"> <p class="aside-title astro-37uy2q7c"> <span class="aside-emoji astro-37uy2q7c" role="img" aria-hidden="true">📝</span> Note </p> <section class="aside-body astro-37uy2q7c"> <p>Under the hood, Jazz’s CoValues are built on <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://jakelazaroff.com/words/an-interactive-intro-to-crdts/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">CRDTs</a> (Conflict-free Replicated Data Types). Unlike Dexie.js where the server handles conflicts, Jazz bakes conflict resolution directly into the data structures — you never have to think about it.</p> </section> </div> </aside> 
<p>Here’s what that looks like in practice. A <code>CoMap</code> tracks every change from every device. When Alice sets <code>completed: false</code> at 8:05 AM and Bob sets <code>completed: true</code> at 8:03 AM, the later timestamp wins. Step through the timeline to see how the resolved state changes as transactions arrive:</p>
<astro-island uid="Z1am0So" component-url="/_astro/CoMapVisualizer.DpWCBExX.js" component-export="default" renderer-url="/_astro/client.DGA1VMK9.js" props="{}" ssr client="only" opts="{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;CoMapVisualizer&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:&quot;react&quot;}"></astro-island>
<h2 id="entry-point-and-build-configuration">Entry Point and Build Configuration<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#entry-point-and-build-configuration"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h2>
<p>The entry point is standard Vue. Update <code>src/main.ts</code>:</p>
<pre class="astro-code tokyo-night" style="background-color:#1a1b26;color:#a9b1d6;overflow-x:auto;white-space:pre-wrap;word-wrap:break-word" tabindex="0" data-language="ts"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> { </span><span style="color:#0DB9D7">createApp</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> }</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> from</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">vue</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#7AA2F7">createApp</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">(</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5">App</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">)</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">.</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7">mount</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">(</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">#app</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">)</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span></code><button type="button" class="copy" data-code="import { createApp } from &#34;vue&#34;;

<p>For Tailwind CSS v4, replace <code>src/assets/main.css</code> with a single import, no <code>tailwind.config.js</code> needed:</p>
<pre class="astro-code tokyo-night" style="background-color:#1a1b26;color:#a9b1d6;overflow-x:auto;white-space:pre-wrap;word-wrap:break-word" tabindex="0" data-language="css"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#9D7CD8">@</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7">import</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">tailwindcss</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span></code><button type="button" class="copy" data-code="@import &#34;tailwindcss&#34;;" onclick="

<p>We also need to tell Vue about the Jazz Inspector custom element so Vue doesn’t try to resolve it as a component. Update <code>vite.config.ts</code>:</p>
<pre class="astro-code tokyo-night" style="background-color:#1a1b26;color:#a9b1d6;overflow-x:auto;white-space:pre-wrap;word-wrap:break-word" tabindex="0" data-language="ts"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> { </span><span style="color:#0DB9D7">fileURLToPath</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">,</span><span style="color:#0DB9D7"> URL</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> }</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> from</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &#39;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">node:url</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&#39;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> { </span><span style="color:#0DB9D7">defineConfig</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> }</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> from</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &#39;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">vite</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&#39;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#0DB9D7"> vue</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> from</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &#39;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">@vitejs/plugin-vue</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&#39;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#0DB9D7"> vueDevTools</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> from</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &#39;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">vite-plugin-vue-devtools</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&#39;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#0DB9D7"> tailwindcss</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> from</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &#39;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">@tailwindcss/vite</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&#39;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">export</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> default</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7"> defineConfig</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">({</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#9ABDF5">    }</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">,</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#9ABDF5">})</span></span></code><button type="button" class="copy" data-code="import { fileURLToPath, URL } from 'node:url'

import vue from '@vitejs/plugin-vue'
import vueDevTools from 'vite-plugin-vue-devtools'
import tailwindcss from '@tailwindcss/vite'

export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [
    vue({
      template: {
        compilerOptions: {
          isCustomElement: (tag) => tag === 'jazz-inspector',
        },
      },
    }),
    vueDevTools(),
    tailwindcss(),
  ],
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@': fileURLToPath(new URL('./src', import.meta.url))
    },
  },
