            navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.dataset.code);
            this.classList.add('copied');
            setTimeout(() => this.classList.remove('copied'), 3000);
          " aria-label="Copy code"><span class="ready"></span><span class="success"></span></button></pre>
<p>The <code>isCustomElement</code> line is important — Jazz ships with a built-in inspector for browsing and debugging CoValues at runtime. It appears as a floating panel where you can click into any CoValue to see its current state, history, and sync status. Since the inspector is a Web Component (<code>&lt;jazz-inspector /&gt;</code>), we need to tell Vue not to resolve it as a Vue component.</p>
<h2 id="setting-up-the-jazz-provider">Setting Up the Jazz Provider<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#setting-up-the-jazz-provider"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h2>
<p>Instead of manually creating a context manager, we use the <code>JazzVueProvider</code> component from <code>community-jazz-vue</code>. It handles context creation, cleanup, and provides Jazz to all child components via Vue’s dependency injection.</p>
<p>Create <code>src/App.vue</code>:</p>
<pre class="astro-code tokyo-night" style="background-color:#1a1b26;color:#a9b1d6;overflow-x:auto;white-space:pre-wrap;word-wrap:break-word" tabindex="0" data-language="vue"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#BA3C97">&lt;</span><span style="color:#F7768E">script</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> setup</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> lang</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">=</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">ts</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> { </span><span style="color:#0DB9D7">ref</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">,</span><span style="color:#0DB9D7"> computed</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> }</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> from</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">vue</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> { </span><span style="color:#0DB9D7">JazzVueProvider</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> }</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> from</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">community-jazz-vue</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">jazz-tools/inspector/register-custom-element</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7DCFFF">import</span><span style="color:#0DB9D7"> TodoApp</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF"> from</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> &quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">./TodoApp.vue</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#9D7CD8;font-style:italic">const</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> isOnline</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7"> ref</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">(</span><span style="color:#FF9E64">true</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">)</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#9D7CD8;font-style:italic">const</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> syncConfig</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7"> computed</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">(()</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> =&gt;</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> ({</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#BA3C97">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#DE5971">JazzVueProvider</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&gt;</span></span>

import { ref, computed } from &#34;vue&#34;;
import { JazzVueProvider } from &#34;community-jazz-vue&#34;;
import &#34;jazz-tools/inspector/register-custom-element&#34;;
import TodoApp from &#34;./TodoApp.vue&#34;;

const isOnline = ref(true);
const syncConfig = computed(() => ({
  peer: &#34;wss://cloud.jazz.tools/?key=vue-jazz-todo-example&#34; as const,
  when: isOnline.value ? (&#34;always&#34; as const) : (&#34;never&#34; as const),
}));
</script>

<template>
  <JazzVueProvider :sync=&#34;syncConfig&#34;>
    <TodoApp v-model:is-online=&#34;isOnline&#34; />
    <jazz-inspector />
  </JazzVueProvider>
</template>" onclick="
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.dataset.code);
            this.classList.add('copied');
            setTimeout(() => this.classList.remove('copied'), 3000);
          " aria-label="Copy code"><span class="ready"></span><span class="success"></span></button></pre>
<p>Three things worth understanding about this setup:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>JazzVueProvider</code> wraps the entire app and takes a <code>sync</code> prop. It only renders children once the Jazz context is ready, so downstream components can safely assume Jazz is available.</li>
<li>The sync config is reactive — the <code>computed</code> derives the config from <code>isOnline</code>. When the user toggles the switch, <code>when</code> flips between <code>&quot;always&quot;</code> and <code>&quot;never&quot;</code>, and Jazz switches between syncing and offline mode.</li>
<li><code>import &quot;jazz-tools/inspector/register-custom-element&quot;</code> registers the <code>&lt;jazz-inspector&gt;</code> Web Component as a side-effect import. The <code>isOnline</code> state lives here and is passed down via <code>v-model:is-online</code>, keeping the sync config and toggle UI separated.</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="building-the-todo-app">Building the Todo App<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#building-the-todo-app"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h2>
<p>Now for the main component. Create <code>src/TodoApp.vue</code> and let’s build it up piece by piece.</p>

<h3 id="routing-via-url">Routing via URL<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#routing-via-url"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h3>
<pre class="astro-code tokyo-night" style="background-color:#1a1b26;color:#a9b1d6;overflow-x:auto;white-space:pre-wrap;word-wrap:break-word" tabindex="0" data-language="ts"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#9D7CD8;font-style:italic">const</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> params</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7"> useUrlSearchParams</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">(</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">history</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">)</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>

const listId = ref<string | undefined>(params.id as string | undefined);

if (!listId.value) {
  const group = Group.create();
  group.addMember(&#34;everyone&#34;, &#34;writer&#34;);
  const newList = ToDoList.create([], { owner: group });
  listId.value = newList.$jazz.id;
  params.id = newList.$jazz.id;
}" onclick="
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.dataset.code);
            this.classList.add('copied');
            setTimeout(() => this.classList.remove('copied'), 3000);
          " aria-label="Copy code"><span class="ready"></span><span class="success"></span></button></pre>
<p>We use VueUse’s <code>useUrlSearchParams(&quot;history&quot;)</code> instead of raw <code>URLSearchParams</code>. The <code>&quot;history&quot;</code> mode uses the History API (no page reload) and gives us a reactive object. If the URL already has an <code>?id=</code> parameter, we subscribe to that existing list. Otherwise, we create a new list owned by a Group with public write access — the same pattern from the permissions section — so anyone with the link can read and write.</p>
<h3 id="subscribing-to-the-list">Subscribing to the List<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#subscribing-to-the-list"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h3>
<pre class="astro-code tokyo-night" style="background-color:#1a1b26;color:#a9b1d6;overflow-x:auto;white-space:pre-wrap;word-wrap:break-word" tabindex="0" data-language="ts"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#9D7CD8;font-style:italic">const</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> todoList</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7"> useCoState</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">(</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5">ToDoList</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">,</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5"> listId</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">,</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#73DACA">  resolve</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">:</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> {</span><span style="color:#73DACA"> $each</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">:</span><span style="color:#FF9E64"> true</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> }</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#9ABDF5">})</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#9D7CD8;font-style:italic">const</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> todos</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7"> computed</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">(()</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> =&gt;</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#9D7CD8;font-style:italic">  const</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> list</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> =</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5"> todoList</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">.</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF">value</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#BB9AF7">  if</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> (</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7">!</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5">list</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">?.</span><span style="color:#7DCFFF">$isLoaded</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">) </span><span style="color:#BB9AF7;font-style:italic">return</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5"> []</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>

  resolve: { $each: true },
});

const todos = computed(() => {
  const list = todoList.value;
  if (!list?.$isLoaded) return [];

<p><code>useCoState</code> is the core composable from <code>community-jazz-vue</code>. It takes a CoValue schema, an ID (which can be a ref), and a resolve query. It returns a Vue <code>Ref</code> that starts as unloaded, populates once available, and re-renders on both local and remote changes.</p>
<p>The <code>resolve: { $each: true }</code> tells Jazz to deeply load each item in the list. Without it, you’d get the list but each ToDo entry would be an unresolved reference. Items are sorted by their <code>order</code> field rather than their position in the CoList.</p>
<p>If you’re interested in how Vue composables like this are designed, I wrote about the patterns here:</p>
<span class="internal-link-wrapper astro-3tyn5ojg"> <a href="/posts/vueuse_composables_style_guide/" class="internal-link astro-3tyn5ojg"> Vue Composables Style Guide: Lessons from VueUse’s Codebase </a> <span class="preview-card astro-3tyn5ojg" role="tooltip"> <span class="preview-content astro-3tyn5ojg"> <span class="preview-title astro-3tyn5ojg">Vue Composables Style Guide: Lessons from VueUse&#39;s Codebase</span> <span class="preview-description astro-3tyn5ojg">A practical guide for writing production-quality Vue 3 composables, distilled from studying VueUse&#39;s patterns for SSR safety, cleanup, and TypeScript.</span> <span class="preview-tags astro-3tyn5ojg"> <span class="preview-tag astro-3tyn5ojg">vue</span><span class="preview-tag astro-3tyn5ojg">typescript</span>  </span> <time class="preview-date astro-3tyn5ojg">Dec 13, 2025</time> </span> </span> </span>  <script>
  function initInternalLinks() {
    const wrappers = document.querySelectorAll(".internal-link-wrapper");

    wrappers.forEach(wrapper => {
      const card = wrapper.querySelector(".preview-card");
      const link = wrapper.querySelector(".internal-link");
      if (!card || !link) return;

      // Skip if already initialized
      if (wrapper.dataset.initialized === "true") return;
      wrapper.dataset.initialized = "true";

      // Function to hide the card
      const hideCard = () => {
        card.classList.remove("is-fixed");
        card.style.removeProperty("--pc-top");
        card.style.removeProperty("--pc-left");
        card.style.opacity = "";
        card.style.visibility = "";
        // Remove scroll listener when hiding
        window.removeEventListener("scroll", hideCard);
      };

      wrapper.addEventListener("mouseenter", () => {
        // Make visible first so it has size
        card.style.opacity = "1";
        card.style.visibility = "visible";

        // Use fixed positioning to escape overflow clipping
        const linkRect = link.getBoundingClientRect();
        const cardRect = card.getBoundingClientRect();

        // Position above by default; flip below if too close to top
        const aboveTop = linkRect.top - 8 - cardRect.height;
        const belowTop = linkRect.bottom + 8;
        const top = aboveTop < 10 ? belowTop : aboveTop;

        // Center horizontally on the link
        const left = linkRect.left + linkRect.width / 2 - cardRect.width / 2;

        // Constrain to viewport
        const vw = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
        const safeLeft = Math.max(8, Math.min(left, vw - cardRect.width - 8));

        // Apply fixed position with coordinates
        card.classList.add("is-fixed");
        card.style.setProperty("--pc-top", `${Math.round(top)}px`);
        card.style.setProperty("--pc-left", `${Math.round(safeLeft)}px`);

        // Hide card on scroll
        window.addEventListener("scroll", hideCard, { passive: true });
      });

      wrapper.addEventListener("mouseleave", hideCard);
    });
  }

  // Initialize on both initial load and after client-side navigation
  document.addEventListener("astro:page-load", initInternalLinks);
</script>

const { focused: inputFocused } = useFocus(inputEl);

function addTodo() {
  const list = todoList.value;
  const title = newTitle.value.trim();
  if (!title || !list?.$isLoaded) return;
  const sorted = todos.value;
  const lastOrder = sorted.length > 0 ? sorted[sorted.length - 1]!.order : null;
  const order = generateKeyBetween(lastOrder, null);
  list.$jazz.push({ title, completed: false, order });
  newTitle.value = &#34;&#34;;
  inputFocused.value = true;
}

function toggleTodo(todo: co.loaded<typeof ToDo>) {
  todo.$jazz.set(&#34;completed&#34;, !todo.completed);
}

function deleteTodo(todo: co.loaded<typeof ToDo>) {
  const list = todoList.value;
  if (!list?.$isLoaded) return;
  const listIndex = [...list].findIndex((t) => t.$jazz.id === todo.$jazz.id);
  if (listIndex !== -1) list.$jazz.remove(listIndex);
}

const copyLink = () => copy(window.location.href);" onclick="
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.dataset.code);
            this.classList.add('copied');
            setTimeout(() => this.classList.remove('copied'), 3000);
          " aria-label="Copy code"><span class="ready"></span><span class="success"></span></button></pre>
<p>Every loaded CoValue exposes a <code>$jazz</code> accessor for mutations — <code>$jazz.push()</code>, <code>$jazz.set()</code>, <code>$jazz.remove()</code>. These mutations are applied locally and synced to all connected peers automatically. No “save” button, no API call.</p>
<p><code>addTodo</code> generates a fractional index via <code>generateKeyBetween(lastOrder, null)</code>, which creates a key that sorts after all existing items. <code>deleteTodo</code> finds the item by its CoValue ID instead of relying on the array index — since our <code>todos</code> computed is sorted by <code>order</code>, the display index won’t match the <code>CoList</code> position.</p>
<h3 id="the-sync-lifecycle">The Sync Lifecycle<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#the-sync-lifecycle"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h3>
<p>Here’s what happens when you call a mutation like <code>list.$jazz.push(...)</code>:</p>
<p><svg id="mermaid-1" width="100%" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" class="flowchart" style="max-width:1632.875px" viewBox="0 0 1632.875 222" role="graphics-document document" aria-roledescription="flowchart-v2"><style>#mermaid-1{font-family:ui-monospace,SFMono-Regular,Menlo,Monaco,Consolas,"Liberation Mono","Courier re-renders</p></span></div></foreignObject></g></g></g></g></g></svg></p>
<p>The mutation returns immediately — your UI updates before the sync even starts. When the data reaches other peers, their <code>useCoState</code> subscriptions fire and Vue re-renders on their end too.</p>
<h2 id="the-todoappvue-template">The TodoApp.vue Template<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#the-todoappvue-template"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h2>
<p>Here’s the complete template that ties together all the script logic — the add form, the sortable list, the online toggle, and the shareable link:</p>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#BA3C97">      &lt;/</span><span style="color:#F7768E">div</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#BA3C97">    &lt;/</span><span style="color:#F7768E">div</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#BA3C97">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#F7768E">div</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#BA3C97">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#F7768E">template</span><span style="color:#BA3C97">&gt;</span></span></code><button type="button" class="copy" data-code="<template>

<p>In the template, <code>:key=&quot;todo.$jazz.id&quot;</code> gives Vue a stable, globally unique key for each item. The <code>ref=&quot;inputEl&quot;</code> connects to <code>useFocus</code> so the input regains focus after adding a todo. And <code>@change=&quot;toggleTodo(todo)&quot;</code> shows how clean mutations are — no actions, no dispatching, no reducers.</p>
<h2 id="drag-and-drop-reordering">Drag-and-Drop Reordering<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#drag-and-drop-reordering"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h2>
<p>We use <a href="https://vueuse.org/integrations/useSortable/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><code>useSortable</code></a> from VueUse for drag-and-drop. The simplest approach would be to call <code>splice</code> on the <code>CoList</code> directly — remove the item from its old position, insert it at the new one. For a single user, that works fine.</p>
<h3 id="the-problem-with-splice">The Problem with <code>splice</code><a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#the-problem-with-splice"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h3>
<p>Jazz’s <code>CoList</code> implements <code>splice</code> as a delete-plus-insert, not as an atomic move. That distinction matters as soon as two users are involved. If both users reorder the same item while offline, each one generates an independent delete-plus-insert. When they sync back up, the list CRDT sees two separate insert operations — and the item appears twice.</p>
<p>This is a fundamental issue with list CRDTs: there’s no “move” operation, only deletes and inserts. So we need a different strategy for ordering.</p>
<h3 id="fractional-indexing-to-the-rescue">Fractional Indexing to the Rescue<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#fractional-indexing-to-the-rescue"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h3>
<p><a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/fractional-indexing" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Fractional indexing</a> (by Rocicorp, based on <a href="https://observablehq.com/@dgreensp/implementing-fractional-indexing" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">this Observable post</a> by David Greenspan) sidesteps the problem entirely. Instead of moving an item in the list, you store an <code>order</code> field on each item and update only that field when reordering. When you move an item between positions A and C, <code>generateKeyBetween(&quot;a&quot;, &quot;c&quot;)</code> returns a key like <code>&quot;b&quot;</code> that sorts between them. The rest of the list stays untouched.</p>
<astro-island uid="Z19XWrE" component-url="/_astro/FractionalIndexingVisualizer.BbZwt6yh.js" component-export="default" renderer-url="/_astro/client.DGA1VMK9.js" props="{}" ssr client="only" opts="{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;FractionalIndexingVisualizer&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:&quot;react&quot;}"></astro-island>
<p>Because <code>order</code> is a field on a <code>CoMap</code>, updates use last-writer-wins semantics. The worst case during a concurrent edit is that one user’s reorder “wins” — but the item never duplicates.</p>
<h3 id="implementation">Implementation<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#implementation"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h3>
<p>Here’s how it looks with <code>useSortable</code>:</p>
<pre class="astro-code tokyo-night" style="background-color:#1a1b26;color:#a9b1d6;overflow-x:auto;white-space:pre-wrap;word-wrap:break-word" tabindex="0" data-language="ts"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#9D7CD8;font-style:italic">const</span><span style="color:#BB9AF7"> todoListEl</span><span style="color:#89DDFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7AA2F7"> useTemplateRef</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&lt;</span><span style="color:#C0CAF5">HTMLElement</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&gt;</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">(</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A">todoListEl</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">&quot;</span><span style="color:#9ABDF5">)</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#9ABDF5">  }</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#9ABDF5">})</span><span style="color:#89DDFF">;</span></span></code><button type="button" class="copy" data-code="const todoListEl = useTemplateRef<HTMLElement>(&#34;todoListEl&#34;);

useSortable(todoListEl, todos, {
  handle: &#34;.drag-handle&#34;,
  animation: 150,
  onUpdate: (e) => {
    // Revert SortableJS DOM manipulation — let Vue re-render from data
    removeNode(e.item);
    insertNodeAt(e.from, e.item, e.oldIndex!);

    const list = todoList.value;
    if (!list?.$isLoaded || e.oldIndex == null || e.newIndex == null) return;

    const sorted = todos.value;
    const before = sorted[e.newIndex - 1]?.order ?? null;
    const after = sorted[e.newIndex + (e.newIndex > e.oldIndex ? 1 : 0)]?.order ?? null;
    const item = sorted[e.oldIndex];
    if (item) item.$jazz.set(&#34;order&#34;, generateKeyBetween(before, after));
  },
});" onclick="
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.dataset.code);
            this.classList.add('copied');
            setTimeout(() => this.classList.remove('copied'), 3000);
          " aria-label="Copy code"><span class="ready"></span><span class="success"></span></button></pre>
<p>The <code>onUpdate</code> handler contains a subtle DOM revert pattern: SortableJS directly manipulates the DOM when the user drags an item, but our source of truth is the <code>order</code> field on each <code>CoMap</code>. So we first undo the DOM change, then update the <code>order</code> field. Vue’s computed re-sorts and re-renders correctly.</p>
<p>The reorder syncs to all peers just like any other mutation. If you’ve worked with cross-tab state syncing before, you’ll know how tricky this can be:</p>
<span class="internal-link-wrapper astro-3tyn5ojg"> <a href="/posts/building-pinia-plugin-cross-tab-sync/" class="internal-link astro-3tyn5ojg"> Building a Pinia Plugin for Cross-Tab State Syncing </a> <span class="preview-card astro-3tyn5ojg" role="tooltip"> <span class="preview-content astro-3tyn5ojg"> <span class="preview-title astro-3tyn5ojg">Building a Pinia Plugin for Cross-Tab State Syncing</span> <span class="preview-description astro-3tyn5ojg">Learn how to create a Pinia plugin that synchronizes state across browser tabs using the BroadcastChannel API and Vue 3&#39;s Script Setup syntax.</span> <span class="preview-tags astro-3tyn5ojg"> <span class="preview-tag astro-3tyn5ojg">vue</span><span class="preview-tag astro-3tyn5ojg">pinia</span>  </span> <time class="preview-date astro-3tyn5ojg">Feb 9, 2025</time> </span> </span> </span>  <script>
  function initInternalLinks() {
    const wrappers = document.querySelectorAll(".internal-link-wrapper");

    wrappers.forEach(wrapper => {
      const card = wrapper.querySelector(".preview-card");
      const link = wrapper.querySelector(".internal-link");
      if (!card || !link) return;

      // Skip if already initialized
      if (wrapper.dataset.initialized === "true") return;
      wrapper.dataset.initialized = "true";

      // Function to hide the card
      const hideCard = () => {
        card.classList.remove("is-fixed");
        card.style.removeProperty("--pc-top");
        card.style.removeProperty("--pc-left");
        card.style.opacity = "";
        card.style.visibility = "";
        // Remove scroll listener when hiding
        window.removeEventListener("scroll", hideCard);
      };

      wrapper.addEventListener("mouseenter", () => {
        // Make visible first so it has size
        card.style.opacity = "1";
        card.style.visibility = "visible";

        // Use fixed positioning to escape overflow clipping
        const linkRect = link.getBoundingClientRect();
        const cardRect = card.getBoundingClientRect();

        // Position above by default; flip below if too close to top
        const aboveTop = linkRect.top - 8 - cardRect.height;
        const belowTop = linkRect.bottom + 8;
        const top = aboveTop < 10 ? belowTop : aboveTop;

        // Center horizontally on the link
        const left = linkRect.left + linkRect.width / 2 - cardRect.width / 2;

        // Constrain to viewport
        const vw = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
        const safeLeft = Math.max(8, Math.min(left, vw - cardRect.width - 8));

        // Apply fixed position with coordinates
        card.classList.add("is-fixed");
        card.style.setProperty("--pc-top", `${Math.round(top)}px`);
        card.style.setProperty("--pc-left", `${Math.round(safeLeft)}px`);

        // Hide card on scroll
        window.addEventListener("scroll", hideCard, { passive: true });
      });

      wrapper.addEventListener("mouseleave", hideCard);
    });
  }

  // Initialize on both initial load and after client-side navigation
  document.addEventListener("astro:page-load", initInternalLinks);
</script>
<h2 id="running-it">Running It<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#running-it"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h2>
<pre class="astro-code tokyo-night" style="background-color:#1a1b26;color:#a9b1d6;overflow-x:auto;white-space:pre-wrap;word-wrap:break-word" tabindex="0" data-language="bash"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C0CAF5">pnpm</span><span style="color:#9ECE6A"> dev</span></span></code><button type="button" class="copy" data-code="pnpm dev" onclick="
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.dataset.code);
            this.classList.add('copied');
            setTimeout(() => this.classList.remove('copied'), 3000);
          " aria-label="Copy code"><span class="ready"></span><span class="success"></span></button></pre>
<p>Open two browser tabs. Add a todo in one, watch it appear instantly in the other. Toggle “Online” off, add more todos, toggle back on — they sync up. Copy the link, open it in an incognito window — same list.</p>
<h2 id="conclusion">Conclusion<a class="heading-link" aria-label="Link to section" href="#conclusion"><span class="heading-link-icon">#</span></a></h2>
<p>The full project is four files of application code:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>src/schema.ts</code> (4 lines) — CoValue definitions</li>
<li><code>src/App.vue</code> (20 lines) — Provider + inspector + online toggle</li>
<li><code>src/TodoApp.vue</code> (~80 lines script + ~125 lines template) — The complete app</li>
<li><code>vite.config.ts</code> (26 lines) — Build config with custom element support</li>
</ul>
<p>What surprised me most coming from the Dexie.js approach is how little code you need. Jazz eliminates the entire backend-sync-API stack. You define your data, mutate it locally, and it syncs.</p>
<p>Two things worth highlighting: fractional indexing for drag-and-drop avoids the duplicate-item problem that <code>CoList</code> splice-based reordering can cause during concurrent offline edits. And Jazz Groups with <code>addMember(&quot;everyone&quot;, &quot;writer&quot;)</code> make the shared URL actually accessible — without this, CoValues are private to the creator.</p>
<p>Check out the <a href="https://jazz.tools" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Jazz documentation</a> for more, and the <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/community-jazz-vue" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">community-jazz-vue package</a> (<a href="https://github.com/garden-co/jazz/tree/main/packages/community-jazz-vue/src" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">source code</a>) for the full Vue API.</p>
<hr/>
<p><strong>Source code:</strong> <a href="https://github.com/alexanderop/vue-jazz-todo-example" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">github.com/alexanderop/vue-jazz-todo-example</a></p>       function initInternalLinks() {
        const wrappers = document.querySelectorAll(".internal-link-wrapper");

        wrappers.forEach(wrapper => {
          const card = wrapper.querySelector(".preview-card");
          const link = wrapper.querySelector(".internal-link");
          if (!card || !link) return;

          // Skip if already initialized
          if (wrapper.dataset.initialized === "true") return;
          wrapper.dataset.initialized = "true";

          // Function to hide the card
          const hideCard = () => {
            card.classList.remove("is-fixed");
            card.style.removeProperty("--pc-top");
            card.style.removeProperty("--pc-left");
            card.style.opacity = "";
            card.style.visibility = "";
            // Remove scroll listener when hiding
            window.removeEventListener("scroll", hideCard);
          };

          wrapper.addEventListener("mouseenter", () => {
            // Make visible first so it has size
            card.style.opacity = "1";
            card.style.visibility = "visible";

            // Use fixed positioning to escape overflow clipping
            const linkRect = link.getBoundingClientRect();
            const cardRect = card.getBoundingClientRect();

            // Position above by default; flip below if too close to top
            const aboveTop = linkRect.top - 8 - cardRect.height;
            const belowTop = linkRect.bottom + 8;
            const top = aboveTop < 10 ? belowTop : aboveTop;

            // Center horizontally on the link
            const left = linkRect.left + linkRect.width / 2 - cardRect.width / 2;

            // Constrain to viewport
            const vw = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
            const safeLeft = Math.max(8, Math.min(left, vw - cardRect.width - 8));

            // Apply fixed position with coordinates
            card.classList.add("is-fixed");
            card.style.setProperty("--pc-top", `${Math.round(top)}px`);
            card.style.setProperty("--pc-left", `${Math.round(safeLeft)}px`);

            // Hide card on scroll
            window.addEventListener("scroll", hideCard, { passive: true });
          });

          wrapper.addEventListener("mouseleave", hideCard);
        });
      }

      // Initialize on both initial load and after client-side navigation
      document.addEventListener("astro:page-load", initInternalLinks);
    </script> </body> </html>  <script>(function(){const postSlug = "building-real-time-todo-app-jazz-vue";

  function updateCTAFollowVisibility() {
    const cta = document.getElementById("cta-follow");
    const article = document.getElementById("article");
    if (!cta || !article) return;

    // If it has the force-hidden class, don't try to show it
    if (cta.classList.contains("force-hidden")) {
      return;
    }

    const viewportHeight = window.innerHeight;
    const articleBottom = article.getBoundingClientRect().bottom;

    // Only show if user has reached the end of the article (article bottom is visible)
    // and hasn't dismissed or subscribed
    if (
      articleBottom <= viewportHeight + 100 && // 100px buffer
      !localStorage.getItem("newsletter_dismissed") &&
      !localStorage.getItem("newsletter_subscribed")
    ) {
      cta.dataset.visible = "true";
      cta.style.transform = "translateX(0)";
      cta.style.opacity = "1";
    } else {
      cta.dataset.visible = "false";
      cta.style.transform = "translateX(-120%)";
      cta.style.opacity = "0";
    }
  }

  // Initialize visibility check
  window.addEventListener("scroll", updateCTAFollowVisibility);
  window.addEventListener("resize", updateCTAFollowVisibility);

  // Add a small delay to initial check to ensure proper positioning
  setTimeout(updateCTAFollowVisibility, 500);

  // Handle newsletter subscribe click with proper tracking
  document
    .getElementById("newsletter-subscribe-button")
    ?.addEventListener("click", () => {
      localStorage.setItem("newsletter_subscribed", "true");

      // Force the popup to stay hidden
      const cta = document.getElementById("cta-follow");
      if (cta) {
        cta.classList.add("force-hidden");
        cta.style.transform = "translateX(-120%)";
        cta.style.opacity = "0";
      }

      if (window.plausible) {
        window.plausible("Newsletter Subscribe Click", {
          props: {
            post: postSlug,
            location: "end_of_article",
            source: "notification",
          },
        });
      }
    });

  // Handle newsletter dismiss click
  document
    .getElementById("newsletter-dismiss")
    ?.addEventListener("click", function () {
      const slug = this.getAttribute("data-post-slug");
      localStorage.setItem("newsletter_dismissed", "true");

      const cta = document.getElementById("cta-follow");
      if (cta) {
        cta.classList.add("force-hidden");
        cta.style.transform = "translateX(-120%)";
        cta.style.opacity = "0";
      }

      if (window.plausible) {
        window.plausible("Newsletter Dismissed", {
          props: {
            post: slug,
            location: "end_of_article",
            source: "notification",
          },
        });
      }
    });
})();</script>  <script>
  /** Create a progress indicator
   *  at the top */
  function createProgressBar() {
    // Create the main container div
    const progressContainer = document.createElement("div");
    progressContainer.className =
      "progress-container fixed top-0 z-10 h-1 w-full bg-skin-fill";

    // Create the progress bar div
    const progressBar = document.createElement("div");
    progressBar.className = "progress-bar h-1 w-0 bg-skin-accent";
    progressBar.id = "myBar";

    // Append the progress bar to the progress container
    progressContainer.appendChild(progressBar);

    // Append the progress container to the document body or any other desired parent element
    document.body.appendChild(progressContainer);
  }
  createProgressBar();

  /** Update the progress bar
   *  when user scrolls */
  function updateScrollProgress() {
    const winScroll =
      document.body.scrollTop || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
    const height =
      document.documentElement.scrollHeight -
      document.documentElement.clientHeight;
    const scrolled = (winScroll / height) * 100;
    const myBar = document.getElementById("myBar");
    if (myBar) {
      myBar.style.width = scrolled + "%";
    }
  }
  document.addEventListener("scroll", updateScrollProgress);

  /** Make headings groups for hover effect on anchor links */
  function makeHeadingsGroups() {
    const headings = Array.from(
      document.querySelectorAll(".prose h2, .prose h3, .prose h4, .prose h5, .prose h6")
    );
    for (const heading of headings) {
      heading.classList.add("group");
    }
  }

  // Run after DOM is loaded
  if (document.readyState === "loading") {
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", makeHeadingsGroups);
  } else {
    makeHeadingsGroups();
  }

  /** Scroll back to top functionality */
  function attachBackToTop() {
    const backToTopBtn = document.getElementById("back-to-top");
    if (backToTopBtn) {
      backToTopBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
        window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: "smooth" });
      });
    }
  }
  attachBackToTop();
</script>
